# NOTES
#  - Bugs in UCA data are NOT FIXED, except for the following problems:
#    - canonical equivalents are decomposed directly (some beta UCA are wrong).
#    - overlapping variable ranges are fixed.
#  - Format is as follows:
#      <codepoint> (' ' <codepoint>)* ';' ('L' | 'S') ';' <fractionalCE>+ ' # ' <UCA_CE> '# ' <name> 
#    - zero weights are not printed
#    - S: contains at least one lowercase or SMALL kana
#    - L: otherwise
#    - Different primaries are separated by a blank line.
# WARNING
#  - Differs from previous version in that MAX value was introduced at 1F.
#    All tertiary values are shifted down by 1, filling the gap at 7!
